Malaga Cove Plaza has everything you need -a nice neighborhood market to grab delicious food or drinks,intersting stores,an impressive Neptune Fountain and peaceful scenery! Take a look,get some things and continue on what many people people call the -"The 17 Mile Drive" of Southern California !

<review>My husband and I shop at this Vons almost exclusively because of it's proximity to our home but also the selection and fair prices. I never thought to leave a review for a grocery store but tonight's visit warranted one. We initially stopped in for the basics but after mulling over what to eat for dinner, we decided to stop by the deli for some chicken. The young man working the deli tonight deserves some very high recognition. His name is Diland and I was beyond impressed with his customer service!

He helped us decide on the best deal for the chicken based on our discussion about quantity and let us know if we downloaded the Vons app, we could get the discount listed on the case (which was a solid $3+ off!). So we did. In the midst of sorting through the app details, he proceeded to bring a cart around to us and said "here you go, you need this more than I do!" He noticed that I was holding a few items in hand and my husband had an overflowing hand basket... not to mention I'm 8 months pregnant so holding anything other than a purse is quite the struggle.

I'm not sure why I was so blown away by his kindness, but I was. Having worked in many customer-facing jobs in the past, I know that sometimes it can get a little monotonous and frustrating to have to ALWAYS be nice, especially when you run into the occasional rude person. So I've felt that over the past few years, customer service has declined in all industries and customers have become more of a burden than someone employees are aiming to please. I have to say, Diland really went above and beyond to not only help us with a good deal, but to provide us with extra comfort that really isn't even part of his job! To say we were impressed is an understatement. He definitely deserves some recognition on here and by his management team. He's got some incredible personal skills that are sometimes hard to find in an employee.

Thank you Diland for putting a smile on our faces tonight :)<//review>< rate>

Update 5/10/17The main issue that needs to be addressed its the poor staffing and their attitudes. I've had issues ever since i could rememberwith this location. The staff in the meat department and deli department are some of the worst, reason being because they will blatantly ignore customers who are quietly waiting to be serviced. She then acted insulted and very disgruntled gave me my bacon. She was giggling and chalking it up on the grey phone for at least five minutes before I had to loudly clear my throat and ask for service. ***
One of the worst Vons in the whole area. The lines waiting here are atrocious (horrible) pretty much any time there are more than ten shoppers in line they get overloaded and the few checkers on duty get flustered easily or seem to be heavily medicated. Courteous butt very slow in most cases. The management it's not on top of things, the deli and bakery personnel specialise in ignoring customers and pretending to look busy our plain out just hiding in the back room area slacking off. My biggest disappointment is the FRESH soups in the front of the store, the deli person could give a damn about checking the fluid levels and temperature of the soups, i come in daily in the evening to get soup and all the pots are burnt, thick, suck to the bottom, crusty and just disgusting. Soups have to be checked every couple hours and water added as needed in the hot tanks. I know, i worked for a cafeteria for years. Also the handicapped stall of the bathroom has been out of service for almost a month now and homeless men Are constantly bathing in the sinks and playing in the stalls. Shame on management. Vons is a disgrace.</review>
